Empty, Queue\nfrom typing import Callable\n\nfrom .gates import gate_passed\nfrom .models import GateCriteria, GateMode, Step\n\n_log = logging.getLogger(\"superclaude.pipeline.trailing_gate\")\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# T05.02 -- GateResultQueue\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass TrailingGateResult:\n    \"\"\"Result of a trailing gate evaluation.\"\"\"\n\n    step_id: str\n    passed: bool\n    evaluation_ms: float\n    failure_reason: str | None = None\n\n\nclass GateResultQueue:\n    \"\"\"Thread-safe queue for collecting gate evaluation results.\n\n    Wraps stdlib ``queue.Queue`` with typed put/drain/pending_count methods.\n    Safe for concurrent access from multiple daemon threads.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self) -> None:\n        self._queue: Queue[TrailingGateResult] = Queue()\n        self._pending = 0\n        self._lock = threading.Lock()\n\n    def put(self, result: TrailingGateResult) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Enqueue a gate result. Thread-safe.\"\"\"\n        self._queue.put(result)\n        with self._lock:\n            self._pending += 1\n\n    def drain(self) -> list[TrailingGateResult]:\n        \"\"\"Collect all available results without blocking.\n\n        Returns a list of all results currently in the queue.\n        \"\"\"\n        results: list[TrailingGateResult] = []\n        while True:\n            try:\n                result = self._queue.get_nowait()\n                results.append(result)\n            except Empty:\n                break\n        with self._lock:\n            self._pending = max(0, self._pending - len(results))\n        return results\n\n    def pending_count(self) -> int:\n        \"\"\"Return count of unprocessed results.\"\"\"\n        return self._queue.qsize()\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# T05.01 -- TrailingGateRunner\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\nclass TrailingGateRunner:\n    \"\"\"Daemon-thread gate evaluator for trailing gate mode.\n\n    Spawns daemon threads to evaluate gate criteria on step output files\n    after the step subprocess completes. Results are collected via the\n    internal GateResultQueue.\n\n    Thread safety: submit() and drain() may be called concurrently from\n    any thread. cancel() propagates to all active daemon threads.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, result_queue: GateResultQueue | None = None) -> None:\n        self._queue = result_queue or GateResultQueue()\n        self._threads: list[threading.Thread] = []\n        self._cancelled = threading.Event()\n        self._pending_count = 0\n        self._lock = threading.Lock()\n\n    @property\n    def result_queue(self) -> GateResultQueue:\n        return self._queue\n\n    def submit(\n        self,\n        step: Step,\n        gate_check: Callable[[Path, GateCriteria], tuple[bool, str | None]] = gate_passed,\n    ) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Spawn a daemon thread to evaluate gate criteria on step output.\n\n        The thread terminates after evaluation completes or cancellation.\n        \"\"\"\n        if step.gate is None:\n            # No gate to evaluate; submit a pass result immediately\n            self._queue.put(\n                TrailingGateResult(\n                    step_id=step.id,\n                    passed=True,\n                    evaluation_ms=0.0,\n                    failure_reason=None,\n                )\n            )\n            return\n\n        with self._lock:\n            self._pending_count += 1\n\n        def _evaluate() -> None:\n            try:\n                if self._cancelled.is_set():\n                    return\n                start = time.monotonic()\n                passed, reason = gate_check(step.output_file, step.gate)\n                elapsed_ms = (time.monotonic() - start) * 1000\n                result = TrailingGateResult(\n                    step_id=step.id,\n                    passed=passed,\n                    evaluation_ms=elapsed_ms,\n                    failure_reason=reason,\n                )\n                self._queue.put(result)\n                _log.debug(\n                    \"Trailing gate for '%s': %s (%.1fms)\",\n                    step.id,\n                    \"PASS\" if passed else \"FAIL\",\n                    elapsed_ms,\n                )\n            except Exception:\n                _log.exception(\"Trailing gate evaluation error for step '%s'\", step.id)\n                self._queue.put(\n                    TrailingGateResult(\n                        step_id=step.id,\n                        passed=False,\n                        evaluation_ms=0.0,\n                        failure_reason=\"Gate evaluation raised an exception\",\n                    )\n                )\n            finally:\n                with self._lock:\n                    self._pending_count -= 1\n\n        t = threading.Thread(target=_evaluate, daemon=True)\n        self._threads.append(t)\n        t.start()\n\n    def drain(self) -> list[TrailingGateResult]:\n        \"\"\"Collect all completed gate results.\"\"\"\n        return self._queue.drain()\n\n    def wait_for_pending(self, timeout: float = 30.0) -> list[TrailingGateResult]:\n        \"\"\"Block until all pending gate evaluations complete or timeout.\n\n        Returns all accumulated results. Never hangs indefinitely.\n        \"\"\"\n        deadline = time.monotonic() + timeout\n        # Join all active threads with bounded timeout\n        for t in list(self._threads):\n            remaining = deadline - time.monotonic()\n            if remaining <= 0:\n                _log.warning(\"wait_for_pending timed out with %d threads still active\", self._pending_count)\n                break\n            t.join(timeout=remaining)\n\n        # Drain whatever results are available\n        return self.drain()\n\n    def cancel(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Signal cancellation to all pending daemon threads.\n\n        Threads check the cancellation event and terminate gracefully.\n        \"\"\"\n        self._cancelled.set()\n        # Give threads a brief window to notice cancellation\n        for t in list(self._threads):\n            t.join(timeout=1.0)\n        self._threads.clear()\n\n    @property\n    def pending_count(self) -> int:\n        \"\"\"Number of gate evaluations still in progress.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            return self._pending_count\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# T05.03 -- DeferredRemediationLog\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# T07.01 -- TrailingGatePolicy Protocol\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\n@runtime_checkable\nclass TrailingGatePolicy(Protocol):\n    \"\"\"Consumer-owned hooks for remediation step construction and file tracking.\n\n    The sprint runner implements this protocol to build remediation steps\n    and detect file changes, decoupling gate infrastructure from sprint-specific\n    logic.\n\n    Methods:\n        build_remediation_step: Construct a focused remediation Step from a gate failure.\n        files_changed: Return the set of file paths modified by a step execution.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def build_remediation_step(self, gate_result: TrailingGateResult) -> Step:\n        \"\"\"Build a remediation Step targeting the specific gate failure.\n\n        Args:\n            gate_result: The failed gate evaluation result.\n\n        Returns:\n            A Step configured to remediate the specific failure.\n        \"\"\"\n        ...\n\n    def files_changed(self, step_result: StepResult) -> set[Path]:\n        \"\"\"Return file paths modified during step execution.\n\n        Args:\n            step_result: The result of executing a step.\n\n        Returns:\n            Set of Path objects for files changed by the step.\n        \"\"\"\n        ...\n\n\nclass RemediationStatus(Enum):\n    \"\"\"Status of a deferred remediation entry.\"\"\"\n\n    PENDING = \"pending\"\n    REMEDIATED = \"remediated\"\n    WAIVED = \"waived\"\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass RemediationEntry:\n    \"\"\"A single deferred remediation record.\"\"\"\n\n self.remediation_status,\n        }\n\n    @classmethod\n    def from_dict(cls, data: dict) -> RemediationEntry:\n        return cls(\n            step_id=data[\"step_id\"],\n            gate_result=data[\"gate_result\"],\n            failure_reason=data[\"failure_reason\"],\n            remediation_status=data.get(\"remediation_status\", RemediationStatus.PENDING.value),\n        )\n\n\nclass DeferredRemediationLog:\n    \"\"\"Persistent log of gate failures requiring remediation.\n\n    Single-writer thread safety: main thread writes, daemon threads may read.\n    Supports RemediationStatus.PENDING.value:\n                    entry.remediation_status = RemediationStatus.REMEDIATED.value\n                    break\n            else:\n                return False\n ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\nclass GateScope(Enum):\n    \"\"\"Scope levels for gate strategy resolution.\"\"\"\n\n    RELEASE = \"release\"\n    MILESTONE = \"milestone\"\n    TASK = \"task\"\n\n\ndef resolve_gate_mode(\n    scope: GateScope,\n    config_gate_mode: GateMode = GateMode.BLOCKING,\n    grace_period: int = 0,\n) -> GateMode:\n    \"\"\"Resolve the effective gate mode based on scope and configuration.\n\n    Rules:\n    - Release scope: ALWAYS BLOCKING (immutable, not configurable)\n    - Milestone scope: configurable, defaults to BLOCKING\n    - Task scope: TRAILING when grace_period > 0, else BLOCKING\n\n    Args:\n        scope: The gate scope level.\n        config_gate_mode: The configured gate mode (used for milestone scope).\n        grace_period: Grace period in seconds (used for task scope).\n\n    Returns:\n        The effective GateMode for this scope.\n    \"\"\"\n    if scope == GateScope.RELEASE:\n        # {self.total_turns_consumed}\",\n            f\"total_duration_seconds: {self.total_duration_seconds:.1f}\",\n            \"tasks:\",\n        ]\n        for tr in self.task_results:\n {self.total_duration_seconds:.1f}s\")\n\n        if self.remaining_task_ids:\n            lines.append(\"\")\n            lines.append(\"## Remaining Tasks (Budget Exhausted)\")\n            for tid CONTINUE\")\n        else:\n            lines.append(\"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\")\n\n        return \"\\n\".join(lines) + \"\\n\"\n\n\ndef aggregate_task_results(\n    phase_number: int,\n    task_results: list[TaskResult],\n    remaining_task_ids: list[str] | None = None,\n    budget_remaining: int = 0,\n) -> AggregatedPhaseReport:\n    \"\"\"Aggregate individual TaskResults into a runner-constructed PhaseReport.\n\n    This function is the runner's authoritative source of task outcomes.\n    It does not rely on agent self-reporting.\n\n    Args:\n        phase_number: The phase number being aggregated.\n        task_results: List of TaskResult from execute_phase_tasks().\n        remaining_task_ids: Task IDs that were not attempted due to budget.\n\n    Returns:\n        AggregatedPhaseReport with computed counts and status.\n    \"\"\"\n    report = AggregatedPhaseReport(\n        phase_number=phase_number,\n        task_results=task_results,\n        remaining_task_ids=remaining_task_ids or [],\n        budget_remaining=budget_remaining,\n    )\n\n    report.tasks_total = len(task_results) + len(report.remaining_task_ids)\n    report.tasks_passed = sum(\n        1 for r in task_results if r.status == TaskStatus.PASS\n    )\n    report.tasks_failed = sum(\n        1 for r in task_results if r.status == TaskStatus.FAIL\n    )\n    report.tasks_incomplete = sum(\n        1 for r in task_results if r.status == TaskStatus.INCOMPLETE\n    )\n    report.tasks_skipped = sum(\n        1 for r in task_results if r.status == TaskStatus.SKIPPED\n    )\n    report.tasks_not_attempted = len(report.remaining_task_ids)\n    report.total_turns_consumed = sum(r.turns_consumed for r in task_results)\n    report.total_duration_seconds = sum(\n        r.duration_seconds for r in task_results\n    )\n\n    return report\n\n\ndef check_budget_guard(ledger: TurnLedger | None) -> str | None:\n    \"\"\"Pre-launch budget guard: returns a halt message if budget is insufficient.\n\n    Returns None if launch is allowed, or a descriptive message string\n    if the budget is too low to launch a subprocess.\n    \"\"\"\n    if ledger is None:\n        return None\n    if ledger.can_launch():\n        return None\n    return (\n        f\"Budget exhausted: {ledger.available()} turns remaining, \"\n        f\"minimum {ledger.minimum_allocation} required for launch\"\n    )\n\n\ndef execute_phase_tasks(\n    tasks: list[TaskEntry],\n    config: SprintConfig,\n    phase,\n    ledger: TurnLedger | None = None,\n    *,\n    _subprocess_factory=None,\n) -> tuple[list[TaskResult], list[str]]:\n    \"\"\"Per-task subprocess orchestration loop.\n\n    Iterates over a task inventory, spawning one subprocess per task with\n    budget allocation from the TurnLedger. Returns task results and a list\n    of remaining (unattempted) task IDs if budget was exhausted.\n\n    Args:\n        tasks: Ordered list of TaskEntry from the tasklist parser.\n        config: Sprint configuration.\n        phase: The Phase being executed.\n        ledger: Optional TurnLedger for budget tracking.\n        _subprocess_factory: Optional callable for testing; signature\n            ``(task, config, phase) -> (exit_code, turns_consumed, output_bytes)``.\n\n    Returns:\n        Tuple of (results, remaining_task_ids). remaining_task_ids is non-empty\n        only when the loop halted due to budget exhaustion.\n    \"\"\"\n    results: list[TaskResult] = []\n    remaining: list[str] = []\n\n    if not tasks:\n        return results, remaining\n\n    for i, task in enumerate(tasks):\n        started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n\n        # Budget check: can we launch?\n        if ledger is not None and not ledger.can_launch():\n            # Mark this and all subsequent tasks as skipped\n            remaining = [t.task_id for t in tasks[i:]]\n            for t in tasks[i:]:\n                results.append(\n                    TaskResult(\n                        task=t,\n                        status=TaskStatus.SKIPPED,\n                        started_at=started_at,\n                        finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n                    )\n                )\n            break\n\n        # Debit the minimum allocation upfront\n        if ledger is not None:\n            ledger.debit(ledger.minimum_allocation)\n\n        # Spawn subprocess for this task\n        if _subprocess_factory is not None:\n            exit_code, turns_consumed, output_bytes = _subprocess_factory(\n                task, config, phase\n            )\n        else:\n            # Default: delegate to ClaudeProcess (real execution)\n            exit_code, turns_consumed, output_bytes = _run_task_subprocess(\n                task, config, phase\n            )\n\n        finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n\n        # Determine task status from exit code\n        if exit_code == 0:\n            status = TaskStatus.PASS\n        elif exit_code == 124:\n            status = TaskStatus.INCOMPLETE\n        else:\n            status = TaskStatus.FAIL\n\n        # Reconcile budget: debit actual consumption, credit back pre-allocation\n        if ledger is not None:\n            # We pre-debited minimum_allocation; now adjust for actual turns\n            actual = max(turns_consumed, 0)\n            pre_allocated = ledger.minimum_allocation\n            if actual > pre_allocated:\n                ledger.debit(actual - pre_allocated)\n            elif actual < pre_allocated:\n                ledger.credit(pre_allocated - actual)\n\n        results.append(\n            TaskResult(\n                task=task,\n                status=status,\n                turns_consumed=turns_consumed,\n                exit_code=exit_code,\n                started_at=started_at,\n                finished_at=finished_at,\n                output_bytes=output_bytes,\n            )\n        )\n\n    return results, remaining\n\n\ndef _run_task_subprocess(\n    task: TaskEntry,\n    config: SprintConfig,\n    phase,\n) -> tuple[int, int, int]:\n    \"\"\"Run a single task in a subprocess. Returns (exit_code, turns, output_bytes).\n\n    This is the real implementation that spawns a ClaudeProcess. For testing,\n    callers of execute_phase_tasks pass _subprocess_factory instead.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Build a task-specific prompt\n    prompt = (\n        f\"Execute task {task.task_id}: {task.title}\\n\"\n        f\"From phase file: {phase.file}\\n\"\n        f\"Description: {task.description}\\n\"\n    )\n\n    proc = ClaudeProcess.__new__(ClaudeProcess)\n    proc.config = config\n    proc.phase = phase\n    from superclaude.cli.pipeline.process import ClaudeProcess as _Base\n    _Base.__init__(\n        proc,\n        prompt=prompt,\n        output_file=config.output_file(phase),\n        error_file=config.error_file(phase),\n        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n        model=config.model,\n        permission_flag=config.permission_flag,\n        timeout_seconds=config.max_turns * 120 + 300,\n        output_format=\"stream-json\",\n    )\n    proc.start()\n    proc.wait()\n    exit_code = proc._process.returncode if proc._process else -1\n    output_path = config.output_file(phase)\n    output_bytes = output_path.stat().st_size if output_path.exists() else 0\n    # Turn counting is wired separately in T02.06\n    return (exit_code if exit_code is not None else -1, 0, output_bytes)\n\n\ndef execute_sprint(config: SprintConfig):\n    \"\"\"Main orchestration loop.\n\n    For each active phase:\n    1. Launch claude -p subprocess\n    2. Start output monitor thread\n    3. Update TUI in a polling loop until process exits (with timeout)\n    4. Parse result file for CONTINUE/HALT\n    5. Record PhaseResult\n    6. Decide whether to continue or halt\n    \"\"\"\n    # Pre-flight: verify claude binary is available before starting TUI/logging\n    if shutil.which(\"claude\") is None:\n        raise SystemExit(\n            \"Error: 'claude' binary not found in PATH. \"\n            \"Install Claude Code CLI before running sprint.\"\n        )\n\n    signal_handler = SignalHandler()\n    signal_handler.install()\n\n    setup_debug_logger(config)\n    import logging as _logging\n    _dbg = _logging.getLogger(_DBG_NAME)\n\n    logger = SprintLogger(config)\n    tui = SprintTUI(config)\n    monitor = OutputMonitor(Path(\"/dev/null\"))  # reset per phase\n    proc_manager: ClaudeProcess | None = None\n\n    sprint_result = SprintResult(config=config)\n    logger.write_header(sprint_result)\n\n    tui.start()\n\n    try:\n        for phase in config.active_phases:\n            if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n                sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n                break\n\n            # Reset monitor for this phase\n            output_path = config.output_file(phase)\n            monitor.reset(output_path)\n            monitor.start()\n\n            # Update tmux tail pane if running in tmux\n            if config.tmux_session_name:\n                update_tail_pane(config.tmux_session_name, output_path)\n\n            # Launch claude\n            proc_manager = ClaudeProcess(config, phase)\n            proc_manager.start()\n            started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n            # Use monotonic clock for deadline enforcement to be immune to NTP adjustments\n            deadline = time.monotonic() + proc_manager.timeout_seconds\n            logger.write_phase_start(phase, started_at)\n\n            debug_log(_dbg, \"PHASE_BEGIN\", phase=phase.number, file=str(phase.file))\n\n            tui.update(sprint_result, monitor.state, phase)\n\n            # Poll loop: wait for process to finish while updating TUI\n            # Enforces monotonic timeout via deadline check.\n            _timed_out = False\n            _stall_acted = False  # single-fire guard for watchdog\n            _poll_start = time.monotonic()\n            while proc_manager._process.poll() is None:\n                if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n                    proc_manager.terminate()\n                    break\n                if time.monotonic() > deadline:\n                    # Timeout reached: kill the process, exit loop\n                    _timed_out = True\n                    proc_manager.terminate()\n                    break\n\n                ms = monitor.state\n                _elapsed = time.monotonic() - _poll_start\n\n                debug_log(\n                    _dbg,\n                    \"poll_tick\",\n                    phase=phase.number,\n                    pid=proc_manager._process.pid,\n                    poll_result=\"running\",\n                    elapsed=round(_elapsed, 1),\n                    output_bytes=ms.output_bytes,\n                    growth_rate=round(ms.growth_rate_bps, 1),\n                    stall_seconds=round(ms.stall_seconds, 1),\n                    stall_status=ms.stall_status,\n                )\n\n                # --- Watchdog: stall timeout check ---\n                if (\n                    config.stall_timeout > 0\n                    and ms.stall_seconds > config.stall_timeout\n                    and ms.events_received > 0  # don't trigger during startup\n                    and not _stall_acted\n                ):\n                    _stall_acted = True\n                    debug_log(\n                        _dbg,\n                        \"watchdog_triggered\",\n                        phase=phase.number,\n                        action=config.stall_action,\n                        stall_seconds=round(ms.stall_seconds, 1),\n                        pid=proc_manager._process.pid,\n                    )\n                    if config.stall_action == \"kill\":\n                        import sys\n                        print(\n                            f\"[WATCHDOG] Stall detected ({ms.stall_seconds:.0f}s > \"\n                            f\"{config.stall_timeout}s) — killing phase {phase.number}\",\n                            file=sys.stderr,\n                        )\n                        _timed_out = True\n                        proc_manager.terminate()\n                        break\n                    else:\n                        # warn action: log and continue\n                        import sys\n                        print(\n                            f\"[WATCHDOG] Stall detected ({ms.stall_seconds:.0f}s > \"\n                            f\"{config.stall_timeout}s) — warning for phase {phase.number}\",\n                            file=sys.stderr,\n                        )\n\n                # Reset single-fire guard when output resumes\n                if _stall_acted and ms.stall_seconds == 0.0:\n                    _stall_acted = False\n\n                # Update TUI at ~2 Hz (monitor thread handles data extraction)\n                # Wrap in try/except so a display glitch cannot abort the sprint\n                try:\n                    tui.update(sprint_result, monitor.state, phase)\n                except Exception as _tui_exc:\n                    import sys\n                    print(f\"[TUI] Display error (continuing sprint): {_tui_exc}\", file=sys.stderr)\n                time.sleep(0.5)\n\n            # If shutdown was requested during the poll loop, classify as\n            # INTERRUPTED rather than letting _determine_phase_status see\n            # exit_code=-1 (None→-1 fallback) and return PhaseStatus.ERROR,\n            # which would incorrectly set the outcome to HALTED.\n            if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n                logger.write_phase_interrupt(phase, started_at, finished_at, exit_code)\n                sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n                break\n\n            # Determine phase status\n            status = _determine_phase_status(\n                exit_code=exit_code,\n                result_file=config.result_file(phase),\n                output_file=config.output_file(phase),\n            )\n\n            # Collect stderr size for telemetry\n            error_file = config.error_file(phase)\n            error_bytes = error_file.stat().st_size if error_file.exists() else 0\n\n            phase_result = PhaseResult(\n                phase=phase,\n                status=status,\n                exit_code=exit_code,\n                started_at=started_at,\n                finished_at=finished_at,\n                output_bytes=monitor.state.output_bytes,\n                error_bytes=error_bytes,\n                last_task_id=monitor.state.last_task_id,\n                files_changed=monitor.state.files_changed,\n            )\n            sprint_result.phase_results.append(phase_result)\n\n            debug_log(\n                _dbg,\n                \"phase_complete\",\n                phase=phase.number,\n                status=status.value,\n                exit_code=exit_code,\n                duration=round(_phase_dur, 1),\n            )\n\n            # Ensure monitor thread and subprocess are cleaned up even on exception.\n        # Each step is independent so one failure does not prevent others.\n        try:\n            monitor.stop()\n        except Exception:\n            pass\n        if proc_manager is not None:\n            try:\n                proc_manager.terminate()\n            except Exception:\n                pass\n        try:\n            tui.stop()\n        except Exception:\n            pass\n        try:\n            signal_handler.uninstall()\n        except Exception:\n            pass\n\n    # Write sentinel exit code file so tmux caller can read the outcome\n    _exitcode = 0 if sprint_result.outcome == SprintOutcome.SUCCESS else 1\n    try:\n        (config.release_dir / \".sprint-exitcode\").write_text(str(_exitcode))\n    except OSError:\n        pass  # best-effort; do not mask the real exit\n\n    if _exitcode != 0:\n        raise SystemExit(_exitcode)\n\n\ndef _determine_phase_status(\n    exit_code: int,\n    result_file: Path,\n    output_file: Path,\n) -> PhaseStatus:\n    \"\"\"Parse result file and exit code to determine phase status.\n\n    Priority:\n    1. Timeout (exit 124) -> TIMEOUT\n    2. Non-zero exit -> ERROR\n    3. Result file with EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT -> HALT\n    4. Result file with EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE -> PASS\n    5. Result file with status: PASS/FAIL -> PASS/HALT\n    6. No result file but output exists -> PASS_NO_REPORT\n    7. No result file and no output -> ERROR\n    \"\"\"\n    if exit_code == 124:\n        return PhaseStatus.TIMEOUT\n    if exit_code != 0:\n        return PhaseStatus.ERROR\n\n    if result_file.exists():\n        content = result_file.read_text(errors=\"replace\")\n        # Use case-insensitive search for EXIT_RECOMMENDATION tokens to handle\n        # model output that varies in casing. When both CONTINUE and HALT appear\n        # (conflicting signals), HALT wins — the stronger/safer outcome.\n        upper = content.upper()\n        has_continue = \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\" in upper\n        has_halt = \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\" in upper\n        if has_halt:\n            return PhaseStatus.HALT\n        if has_continue:\n            return PhaseStatus.PASS\n        if re.search(r\"status:\\s*PASS\\b\", content, re.IGNORECASE):\n            return PhaseStatus.PASS\n        if re.search(r\"status:\\s*FAIL(?:ED|URE)?\\b\", content, re.IGNORECASE):\n            return PhaseStatus.HALT\n        # PARTIAL result means tasks did not fully complete — treat as halt\n        if re.search(r\"status:\\s*PARTIAL\\b\", content, re.IGNORECASE):\n            return PhaseStatus.HALT\n        return PhaseStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL\n\n    if output_file.exists() and output_file.stat().st_size > 0:\n        # Check for budget exhaustion: a subprocess that exits 0 but hit\n        # error_max_turns produced no useful result — reclassify as INCOMPLETE\n        # to trigger HALT instead of silent continuation.\n        if detect_error_max_turns(output_file):\n            return PhaseStatus.INCOMPLETE\n        return PhaseStatus.PASS_NO_REPORT\n\n    return PhaseStatus.ERROR\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":31,"oldLines":6,"newStart":31,"newLines":9,"lines":[" from .tmux import update_tail_pane"," from .tui import SprintTUI"," ","+from superclaude.cli.pipeline.models import Step, StepResult","+from superclaude.cli.pipeline.trailing_gate import TrailingGatePolicy, TrailingGateResult","+"," # Debug logger name for executor-specific events"," _DBG_NAME = \"superclaude.sprint.debug.executor\""," "]}],"userModified":false,"replaceAll":false}}

---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# 4-Layer Subprocess Isolation\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n@dataclass\nclass IsolationLayers:\n    \"\"\"Configuration for the 4-layer subprocess isolation.\n\n    Each layer prevents cross-task state leakage:\n    1. scoped_work_dir: Restrict working directory to release dir\n    2. git_boundary: Set GIT_CEILING_DIRECTORIES to prevent upward traversal\n    3. empty_plugin_dir: Point CLAUDE_PLUGIN_DIR to an empty tempdir\n    4. restricted_settings: Set CLAUDE_SETTINGS_DIR to an isolated tempdir\n\n    The ``env_vars`` property returns a dict of environment variable overrides\n    that should be merged into the subprocess environment.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    scoped_work_dir: Path\n    git_boundary: Path\n    plugin_dir: Path\n    settings_dir: Path\n\n    @property\n    def env_vars(self) -> dict[str, str]:\n        \"\"\"Return environment variable overrides for all 4 isolation layers.\"\"\"\n        return {\n            \"CLAUDE_WORK_DIR\": str(self.settings_dir),\n        }\n\n    @property\n    def layers_active(self) -> list[str]:\n        \"\"\"Return list of active isolation layer names for verification.\"\"\"\n        active = []\n setup_isolation(config: SprintConfig) -> IsolationLayers:\n    \"\"\"Create 4-layer isolation for subprocess execution.\n\n    Sets up:\n    1. Scoped working directory (the release dir)\n    2. Git boundary (prevents git operations above release dir)\n    3. Empty plugin directory (no plugins loaded)\n    4. Restricted settings directory (minimal settings)\n\n    All directories are created if they don't exist. Aggregation — runner-constructed phase reports\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n@dataclass\nclass AggregatedPhaseReport:\n    \"\"\"Runner-constructed phase report from collected TaskResults.\n\n    This report is built by the runner, not by parsing agent self-reported\n    output, ensuring accurate task outcome tracking even when subprocesses\n    are budget-exhausted.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    phase_number: int\n    tasks_total: int = 0\n    tasks_passed: int = 0\n    tasks_failed: int = 0\n    tasks_incomplete: int = 0\n    tasks_skipped: int = 0\n field(default_factory=list)\n    remaining_task_ids: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)\n\n    @property\n    def status(self) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Overall phase status: PASS, FAIL, or PARTIAL.\"\"\"\n        if self.tasks_total == 0:\n            return \"PASS\"\n        if self.tasks_passed == self.tasks_total:\n            return \"PASS\"\n        if self.tasks_passed == 0:\n            return \"FAIL\"\n        return \"PARTIAL\"\n\n    def to_yaml(self) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Render the report as a YAML string.\n\n        Produces a machine-readable YAML document with standardized fields\n        for downstream tooling and TUI display.\n        \"\"\"\n        lines = [\n            f\"phase: {self.phase_number}\",\n            f\"status: {self.status}\",\n            f\"tasks_total: {self.tasks_total}\",\n            f\"tasks_passed: {self.tasks_passed}\",\n            f\"tasks_failed: {self.tasks_failed}\",\n            f\"tasks_incomplete: {self.tasks_incomplete}\",\n            f\"tasks_not_attempted: {self.tasks_not_attempted}\",\n            f\"budget_remaining: {self.budget_remaining}\",\n            f\"total_turns_consumed: {self.total_turns_consumed}\",\n            f\"total_duration_seconds: {self.total_duration_seconds:.1f}\",\n            \"tasks:\",\n        ]\n        for tr in self.task_results:\n            lines.append(f\"  - task_id: {tr.task.task_id}\")\n            lines.append(f\"    title: \\\"{tr.task.title}\\\"\")\n            lines.append(f\"    status: {tr.status.value}\")\n            lines.append(f\"    gate_outcome: {tr.gate_outcome.value}\")\n            lines.append(f\"    turns_consumed: {tr.turns_consumed}\")\n            lines.append(f\"    duration_seconds: {tr.duration_seconds:.1f}\")\n        if self.remaining_task_ids:\n            lines.append(\"remaining_tasks:\")\n            for tid in self.remaining_task_ids:\n                lines.append(f\"  - {tid}\")\n        return \"\\n\".join(lines) + \"\\n\"\n\n    def to_markdown(self) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Render the report as a markdown string with YAML frontmatter.\"\"\"\n        lines = [\n            \"---\",\n            f\"phase: {self.phase_number}\",\n            f\"status: {self.status}\",\n            f\"tasks_total: {self.tasks_total}\",\n            f\"tasks_passed: {self.tasks_passed}\",\n            f\"tasks_failed: {self.tasks_failed}\",\n            \"---\",\n            \"\",\n            f\"# Phase {self.phase_number} — Aggregated Task Report\",\n            \"\",\n            \"| Task ID | Title | Status | Turns | Duration |\",\n            \"|---------|-------|--------|-------|----------|\",\n        ]\n        for tr in self.task_results:\n            dur = f\"{tr.duration_seconds:.1f}s\"\n            lines.append(\n                f\"| {tr.task.task_id} | {tr.task.title} | {tr.status.value} \"\n                f\"| {tr.turns_consumed} | {dur} |\"\n            )\n        lines.append(\"\")\n        lines.append(f\"**Total turns consumed:** {self.total_turns_consumed}\")\n        lines.append(f\"**Total duration:** {self.total_duration_seconds:.1f}s\")\n\n        if self.remaining_task_ids:\n            lines.append(\"\")\n            lines.append(\"## Remaining Tasks (Budget Exhausted)\")\n            for tid in self.remaining_task_ids:\n                lines.append(f\"- {tid}\")\n\n        lines.append(\"\")\n        if self.status == \"PASS\":\n            lines.append(\"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\")\n        else:\n            lines.append(\"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\")\n\n        return \"\\n\".join(lines) + \"\\n\"\n\n\ndef aggregate_task_results(\n    phase_number: int,\n    task_results: list[TaskResult],\n    remaining_task_ids: list[str] | None = None,\n    budget_remaining: int = 0,\n) -> AggregatedPhaseReport:\n    \"\"\"Aggregate individual TaskResults into a runner-constructed PhaseReport.\n\n    This function is the runner's authoritative source of task outcomes.\n    It does not rely on agent self-reporting.\n\n    Args:\n        phase_number: The phase number being aggregated.\n        task_results: List of TaskResult from execute_phase_tasks().\n        remaining_task_ids: Task IDs that were not attempted due to budget.\n\n    Returns:\n        AggregatedPhaseReport with computed counts and status.\n    \"\"\"\n    report = AggregatedPhaseReport(\n        phase_number=phase_number,\n        task_results=task_results,\n        remaining_task_ids=remaining_task_ids or [],\n        budget_remaining=budget_remaining,\n    )\n\n    report.tasks_total = len(task_results) + len(report.remaining_task_ids)\n    report.tasks_passed = sum(\n        1 for r in task_results if r.status == TaskStatus.PASS\n    )\n    report.tasks_failed = sum(\n        1 for r in task_results if r.status == TaskStatus.FAIL\n    )\n    report.tasks_incomplete = sum(\n        1 for r in task_results if r.status == TaskStatus.INCOMPLETE\n    )\n    report.tasks_skipped = sum(\n        1 for r in task_results if r.status == TaskStatus.SKIPPED\n    )\n    report.tasks_not_attempted = len(report.remaining_task_ids)\n    report.total_turns_consumed = sum(r.turns_consumed for r in task_results)\n    report.total_duration_seconds = sum(\n        r.duration_seconds for r in task_results\n    )\n\n    return report\n\n\ndef check_budget_guard(ledger: TurnLedger | None) -> str | None:\n    \"\"\"Pre-launch budget guard: returns a halt message if budget is insufficient.\n\n    Returns None if launch is allowed, or a descriptive message string\n    if the budget is too low to launch a subprocess.\n    \"\"\"\n    if ledger is None:\n        return None\n    if ledger.can_launch():\n        return None\n    return (\n        f\"Budget exhausted: {ledger.available()} turns remaining, \"\n        f\"minimum {ledger.minimum_allocation} required for launch\"\n    )\n\n\ndef execute_phase_tasks(\n    tasks: list[TaskEntry],\n    config: SprintConfig,\n    phase,\n    ledger: TurnLedger | None = None,\n    *,\n    _subprocess_factory=None,\n) -> tuple[list[TaskResult], list[str]]:\n    \"\"\"Per-task subprocess orchestration loop.\n\n    Iterates over a task inventory, spawning one subprocess per task with\n    budget allocation from the TurnLedger. Returns task results and a list\n    of remaining (unattempted) task IDs if budget was exhausted.\n\n    Args:\n        tasks: Ordered list of TaskEntry from the tasklist parser.\n        config: Sprint configuration.\n        phase: The Phase being executed.\n        ledger: Optional TurnLedger for budget tracking.\n        _subprocess_factory: Optional callable for testing; signature\n            ``(task, config, phase) -> (exit_code, turns_consumed, output_bytes)``.\n\n    Returns:\n        Tuple of (results, remaining_task_ids). remaining_task_ids is non-empty\n        only when the loop halted due to budget exhaustion.\n    \"\"\"\n    results: list[TaskResult] = []\n    remaining: list[str] = []\n\n    if not tasks:\n        return results, remaining\n\n    for i, task in enumerate(tasks):\n        started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n\n        # Budget check: can we launch?\n        if ledger is not None and not ledger.can_launch():\n            # Mark this and all subsequent tasks as skipped\n            remaining = [t.task_id for t in tasks[i:]]\n            for t in tasks[i:]:\n                results.append(\n                    TaskResult(\n                        task=t,\n                        status=TaskStatus.SKIPPED,\n                        started_at=started_at,\n                        finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n                    )\n                )\n            break\n\n        # Debit the minimum allocation upfront\n        if ledger is not None:\n            ledger.debit(ledger.minimum_allocation)\n\n        # Spawn subprocess for this task\n        if _subprocess_factory is not None:\n            exit_code, turns_consumed, output_bytes = _subprocess_factory(\n                task, config, phase\n            )\n        else:\n            # Default: delegate to ClaudeProcess (real execution)\n            exit_code, turns_consumed, output_bytes = _run_task_subprocess(\n                task, config, phase\n            )\n\n        finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n\n        # Determine task status from exit code\n        if exit_code == 0:\n            status = TaskStatus.PASS\n        elif exit_code == 124:\n            status = TaskStatus.INCOMPLETE\n        else:\n            status = TaskStatus.FAIL\n\n        # Reconcile budget: debit actual consumption, credit back pre-allocation\n        if ledger is not None:\n            # We pre-debited minimum_allocation; now adjust for actual turns\n            actual = max(turns_consumed, 0)\n            pre_allocated = ledger.minimum_allocation\n            if actual > pre_allocated:\n                ledger.debit(actual - pre_allocated)\n            elif actual < pre_allocated:\n                ledger.credit(pre_allocated - actual)\n\n        results.append(\n            TaskResult(\n                task=task,\n                status=status,\n                turns_consumed=turns_consumed,\n                exit_code=exit_code,\n                started_at=started_at,\n                finished_at=finished_at,\n                output_bytes=output_bytes,\n            )\n        )\n\n    return results, remaining\n\n\ndef _run_task_subprocess(\n    task: TaskEntry,\n    config: SprintConfig,\n    phase,\n) -> tuple[int, int, int]:\n    \"\"\"Run a single task in a subprocess. Returns (exit_code, turns, output_bytes).\n\n    This is the real implementation that spawns a ClaudeProcess. For testing,\n    callers of execute_phase_tasks pass _subprocess_factory instead.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Build a task-specific prompt\n    prompt = (\n        f\"Execute task {task.task_id}: {task.title}\\n\"\n        f\"From phase file: {phase.file}\\n\"\n        f\"Description: {task.description}\\n\"\n    )\n\n    proc = ClaudeProcess.__new__(ClaudeProcess)\n    proc.config = config\n    proc.phase = phase\n    from superclaude.cli.pipeline.process import ClaudeProcess as _Base\n    _Base.__init__(\n        proc,\n        prompt=prompt,\n        output_file=config.output_file(phase),\n        error_file=config.error_file(phase),\n        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n        model=config.model,\n        permission_flag=config.permission_flag,\n        timeout_seconds=config.max_turns * 120 + 300,\n        output_format=\"stream-json\",\n    )\n    proc.start()\n    proc.wait()\n    exit_code = proc._process.returncode if proc._process else -1\n    output_path = config.output_file(phase)\n    output_bytes = output_path.stat().st_size if output_path.exists() else 0\n    # Turn counting is wired separately in T02.06\n    return (exit_code if exit_code is not None else -1, 0, output_bytes)\n\n\ndef execute_sprint(config: SprintConfig):\n    \"\"\"Main orchestration loop.\n\n    For each active phase:\n    1. Launch claude -p subprocess\n    2. Start output monitor thread\n    3. Update TUI in a polling loop until process exits (with timeout)\n    4. Parse result file for CONTINUE/HALT\n    5. Record PhaseResult\n    6. Decide whether to continue or halt\n    \"\"\"\n    # Pre-flight: verify claude binary is available before starting TUI/logging\n    if shutil.which(\"claude\") is None:\n        raise SystemExit(\n            \"Error: 'claude' binary not found in PATH. \"\n            \"Install Claude Code CLI before running sprint.\"\n        )\n\n    signal_handler = SignalHandler()\n    signal_handler.install()\n\n    setup_debug_logger(config)\n    import logging as _logging\n    _dbg = _logging.getLogger(_DBG_NAME)\n\n    logger = SprintLogger(config)\n    tui = SprintTUI(config)\n    monitor = OutputMonitor(Path(\"/dev/null\"))  # reset per phase\n    proc_manager: ClaudeProcess | None = None\n\n    sprint_result = SprintResult(config=config)\n    logger.write_header(sprint_result)\n\n    tui.start()\n\n    try:\n        for phase in config.active_phases:\n            if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n                sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n                break\n\n            # Reset monitor for this phase\n            output_path = config.output_file(phase)\n            monitor.reset(output_path)\n            monitor.start()\n\n            # Update tmux tail pane if running in tmux\n            if config.tmux_session_name:\n                update_tail_pane(config.tmux_session_name, output_path)\n\n            # Launch claude\n            proc_manager = ClaudeProcess(config, phase)\n            proc_manager.start()\n            started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n            # Use monotonic clock for deadline enforcement to be immune to NTP adjustments\n            deadline = time.monotonic() + proc_manager.timeout_seconds\n            logger.write_phase_start(phase, started_at)\n\n            debug_log(_dbg, \"PHASE_BEGIN\", phase=phase.number, file=str(phase.file))\n\n            tui.update(sprint_result, monitor.state, phase)\n\n            # Poll loop: wait for process to finish while updating TUI\n            # Enforces monotonic timeout via deadline check.\n            _timed_out = False\n            _stall_acted = False  # single-fire guard for watchdog\n            _poll_start = time.monotonic()\n            while proc_manager._process.poll() is None:\n                if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n                    proc_manager.terminate()\n                    break\n                if time.monotonic() > deadline:\n                    # Timeout reached: kill the process, exit loop\n                    _timed_out = True\n                    proc_manager.terminate()\n                    break\n\n                ms = monitor.state\n                _elapsed = time.monotonic() - _poll_start\n\n                debug_log(\n                    _dbg,\n                    \"poll_tick\",\n                    phase=phase.number,\n                    pid=proc_manager._process.pid,\n                    poll_result=\"running\",\n                    elapsed=round(_elapsed, 1),\n                    output_bytes=ms.output_bytes,\n                    growth_rate=round(ms.growth_rate_bps, 1),\n                    stall_seconds=round(ms.stall_seconds, 1),\n                    stall_status=ms.stall_status,\n                )\n\n                # --- Watchdog: stall timeout check ---\n                if (\n                    config.stall_timeout > 0\n                    and ms.stall_seconds > config.stall_timeout\n                    and ms.events_received > 0  # don't trigger during startup\n                    and not _stall_acted\n                ):\n                    _stall_acted = True\n                    debug_log(\n                        _dbg,\n                        \"watchdog_triggered\",\n                        phase=phase.number,\n                        action=config.stall_action,\n                        stall_seconds=round(ms.stall_seconds, 1),\n                        pid=proc_manager._process.pid,\n                    )\n                    if config.stall_action == \"kill\":\n                        import sys\n                        print(\n                            f\"[WATCHDOG] Stall detected ({ms.stall_seconds:.0f}s > \"\n                            f\"{config.stall_timeout}s) — killing phase {phase.number}\",\n                            file=sys.stderr,\n                        )\n                        _timed_out = True\n                        proc_manager.terminate()\n                        break\n                    else:\n                        # warn action: log and continue\n                        import sys\n                        print(\n                            f\"[WATCHDOG] Stall detected ({ms.stall_seconds:.0f}s > \"\n                            f\"{config.stall_timeout}s) — warning for phase {phase.number}\",\n                            file=sys.stderr,\n                        )\n\n                # Reset single-fire guard when output resumes\n                if _stall_acted and ms.stall_seconds == 0.0:\n                    _stall_acted = False\n\n                # Update TUI at ~2 Hz (monitor thread handles data extraction)\n                # Wrap in try/except so a display glitch cannot abort the sprint\n                try:\n                    tui.update(sprint_result, monitor.state, phase)\n                except Exception as _tui_exc:\n                    import sys\n                    print(f\"[TUI] Display error (continuing sprint): {_tui_exc}\", file=sys.stderr)\n                time.sleep(0.5)\n\n            # Safely read exit code: returncode may be None if terminate raced.\n            # Use _timed_out flag instead of assigning directly to returncode.\n            raw_rc = proc_manager._process.returncode\n            if _timed_out:\n                exit_code = 124\n            else:\n                exit_code = raw_rc if raw_rc is not None else -1\n            monitor.stop()\n            finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n            _phase_dur = (finished_at - started_at).total_seconds()\n            debug_log(\n                _dbg,\n                \"PHASE_END\",\n                phase=phase.number,\n                exit_code=exit_code,\n                duration=round(_phase_dur, 1),\n            )\n\n            # If shutdown was requested during the poll loop, classify as\n            # INTERRUPTED rather than letting _determine_phase_status see\n            # exit_code=-1 (None→-1 fallback) and return PhaseStatus.ERROR,\n            # which would incorrectly set the outcome to HALTED.\n            if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n                logger.write_phase_interrupt(phase, started_at, finished_at, exit_code)\n                sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n                break\n\n            # Determine phase status\n            status = _determine_phase_status(\n                exit_code=exit_code,\n                result_file=config.result_file(phase),\n                output_file=config.output_file(phase),\n            )\n\n            # Collect stderr size for telemetry\n            error_file = config.error_file(phase)\n            error_bytes = error_file.stat().st_size if error_file.exists() else 0\n\n            phase_result = PhaseResult(\n                phase=phase,\n                status=status,\n                exit_code=exit_code,\n                started_at=started_at,\n                finished_at=finished_at,\n                output_bytes=monitor.state.output_bytes,\n                error_bytes=error_bytes,\n                last_task_id=monitor.state.last_task_id,\n                files_changed=monitor.state.files_changed,\n            )\n            sprint_result.phase_results.append(phase_result)\n\n            debug_log(\n                _dbg,\n                \"phase_complete\",\n                phase=phase.number,\n                status=status.value,\n                exit_code=exit_code,\n                duration=round(_phase_dur, 1),\n            )\n\n            # Log and notify\n            logger.write_phase_result(phase_result)\n            notify_phase_complete(phase_result)\n\n            tui.update(sprint_result, monitor.state, None)\n\n            # Decide: continue or halt?\n            if status.is_failure:\n                # Collect diagnostics for the failed phase\n                try:\n                    collector = DiagnosticCollector(config)\n                    bundle = collector.collect(phase, phase_result, monitor.state)\n                    classifier = FailureClassifier()\n                    bundle.category = classifier.classify(bundle)\n                    reporter = ReportGenerator()\n                    diag_path = config.results_dir / f\"phase-{phase.number}-diagnostic.md\"\n                    reporter.write(bundle, diag_path)\n                    debug_log(\n                        _dbg,\n                        \"diagnostic_report\",\n                        phase=phase.number,\n                        category=bundle.category.value,\n                        path=str(diag_path),\n                    )\n                except Exception as _diag_exc:\n                    debug_log(_dbg, \"diagnostic_error\", phase=phase.number, error=str(_diag_exc))\n\n                sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.HALTED\n                sprint_result.halt_phase = phase.number\n                break\n\n        # Sprint finished\n        sprint_result.finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n        if sprint_result.outcome == SprintOutcome.SUCCESS:\n            # Verify all phases actually passed\n            if not all(r.status.is_success for r in sprint_result.phase_results):\n                sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.ERROR\n\n        tui.update(sprint_result, MonitorState(), None)\n        logger.write_summary(sprint_result)\n        notify_sprint_complete(sprint_result)\n\n    finally:\n        # Ensure monitor thread and subprocess are cleaned up even on exception.\n        # Each step is independent so one failure does not prevent others.\n        try:\n            monitor.stop()\n        except Exception:\n            pass\n        if proc_manager is not None:\n            try:\n                proc_manager.terminate()\n            except Exception:\n                pass\n        try:\n            tui.stop()\n        except Exception:\n            pass\n        try:\n            signal_handler.uninstall()\n        except Exception:\n            pass\n\n    # Write sentinel exit code file so tmux caller can read the outcome\n    _exitcode = 0 if sprint_result.outcome == SprintOutcome.SUCCESS else 1\n    try:\n        (config.release_dir / \".sprint-exitcode\").write_text(str(_exitcode))\n    except OSError:\n        pass  # best-effort; do not mask the real exit\n\n    if _exitcode != 0:\n        raise SystemExit(_exitcode)\n\n\ndef _determine_phase_status(\n    exit_code: int,\n    result_file: Path,\n    output_file: Path,\n) -> PhaseStatus:\n    \"\"\"Parse result file and exit code to determine phase status.\n\n    Priority:\n    1. Timeout (exit 124) -> TIMEOUT\n    2. Non-zero exit -> ERROR\n    3. Result file with EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT -> HALT\n    4. Result file with EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE -> PASS\n    5. Result file with status: PASS/FAIL -> PASS/HALT\n    6. No result file but output exists -> PASS_NO_REPORT\n    7. No result file and no output -> ERROR\n    \"\"\"\n    if exit_code == 124:\n        return PhaseStatus.TIMEOUT\n    if exit_code != 0:\n        return PhaseStatus.ERROR\n\n    if result_file.exists():\n        content = result_file.read_text(errors=\"replace\")\n        # Use case-insensitive search for EXIT_RECOMMENDATION tokens to handle\n        # model output that varies in casing. When both CONTINUE and HALT appear\n        # (conflicting signals), HALT wins — the stronger/safer outcome.\n        upper = content.upper()\n        has_continue = \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\" in upper\n        has_halt = \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\" in upper\n        if has_halt:\n            return PhaseStatus.HALT\n        if has_continue:\n            return PhaseStatus.PASS\n        if re.search(r\"status:\\s*PASS\\b\", content, re.IGNORECASE):\n            return PhaseStatus.PASS\n        if re.search(r\"status:\\s*FAIL(?:ED|URE)?\\b\", content, re.IGNORECASE):\n            return PhaseStatus.HALT\n        # PARTIAL result means tasks did not fully complete — treat as halt\n        if re.search(r\"status:\\s*PARTIAL\\b\", content, re.IGNORECASE):\n            return TestGateResultQueue:\n    \"\"\"Thread-safe queue for gate results.\"\"\"\n\n    def test_put_and_drain(self):\n        q = GateResultQueue()\n        r = TrailingGateResult(step_id=\"s1\", passed=True, evaluation_ms=1.0)\n        q.put(r)\n        results = q.drain()\n        assert len(results) == 1\n        assert results[0].step_id == \"s1\"\n        assert results[0].passed is True\n\n    def test_drain_empty(self):\n        q = GateResultQueue()\n        results = q.drain()\n        assert results == []\n\n    def test_pending_count(self):\n        q = GateResultQueue()\n        assert q.pending_count() == 0\n        q.put(TrailingGateResult(step_id=\"s1\", passed=True, evaluation_ms=1.0))\n        assert q.pending_count() == 1\n        q.put(TrailingGateResult(step_id=\"s2\", passed=False, evaluation_ms=2.0))\n        assert q.pending_count() == 2\n        q.drain()\n        assert q.pending_count() == 0\n\n    def test_concurrent_put_drain(self):\n        \"\"\"Thread-safe under concurrent access from >=3 threads.\"\"\"\n        q = GateResultQueue()\n        results_collected: list[TrailingGateResult] = []\n        errors: list[str] = []\n\n        def producer(start_id: int, count: int):\n            for i in range(count):\n                q.put(TrailingGateResult(\n  # let producers get ahead\n            while True:\n                batch = q.drain()\n                if batch:\n                    collected.extend(batch)\n                else:\n                    break\n\n        # 3 producer threads, each producing 10 results\n        threads = [\n            threading.Thread(target=producer, args=(0, 10)),\n            threading.Thread(target=producer, args=(100, 10)),\n            threading.Thread(target=producer, args=(200, 10)),\n        ]\n        for t in threads:\n            t.start()\n        for t in threads:\n            t.join()\n\n        # Drain all results\n        final = q.drain()\n        assert len(final) == 30  # All 30 results collected without loss\n\n    def test_results_associated_with_correct_step_id(self):\n        q.put(TrailingGateResult(step_id=\"beta\", passed=False, evaluation_ms=2.0, failure_reason=\"bad\"))\n        results = q.drain()\n        by_id = {r.step_id: r for r in results}\n             step_id=f\"w-{i}\", passed=False,\n                    evaluation_ms=float(i), failure_reason=f\"fail-{i}\",\n                ))\n\n        def reader():\n            for _ in range(20):\n       r1 = threading.Thread(target=reader)\n        r2 = threading.Thread(target=reader)\n        w.start()\n        r1.start()\n        r2.start()\n        w.join()\n        r1.join()\n        r2.join()\n\n        assert len(errors) == 0\n        assert log.entry_count == 20\n\n\n# ===========================================================================\n# T05.04 -- Scope-Based Gate logging\nimport threading\nimport time\nfrom dataclasses import asdict, dataclass, field\nfrom enum import Enum\nfrom pathlib import Path\nfrom queue import Empty, Queue\nfrom typing import Callable, Protocol, runtime_checkable\n\nfrom .gates import gate_passed\nfrom .models import GateCriteria, GateMode, Step, StepResult\n\n_log = logging.getLogger(\"superclaude.pipeline.trailing_gate\")\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# T05.02 -- GateResultQueue\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass TrailingGateResult:\n    \"\"\"Result of a trailing gate evaluation.\"\"\"\n\n    step_id: str\n    passed: bool\n    evaluation_ms: float\n    failure_reason: str | None = None\n\n\nclass GateResultQueue:\n    \"\"\"Thread-safe queue for collecting gate evaluation results.\n\n    Wraps stdlib ``queue.Queue`` with typed put/drain/pending_count methods.\n    Safe for concurrent access from multiple daemon threads.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self) -> None:\n        self._queue: Queue[TrailingGateResult] = Queue()\n        self._pending = 0\n        self._lock = threading.Lock()\n\n    def put(self, result: TrailingGateResult) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Enqueue a gate result. Thread-safe.\"\"\"\n        self._queue.put(result)\n        with self._lock:\n            self._pending += 1\n\n    def drain(self) -> list[TrailingGateResult]:\n        \"\"\"Collect all available results without blocking.\n\n        Returns a list of all results currently in the queue.\n        \"\"\"\n        results: list[TrailingGateResult] = []\n        while True:\n            try:\n                result = self._queue.get_nowait()\n                results.append(result)\n            except Empty:\n                break\n        with self._lock:\n            self._pending = max(0, self._pending - len(results))\n        return results\n\n    def pending_count(self) -> int:\n        \"\"\"Return count of unprocessed results.\"\"\"\n        return self._queue.qsize()\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# T05.01 -- TrailingGateRunner\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\nclass TrailingGateRunner:\n    \"\"\"Daemon-thread gate evaluator for trailing gate mode.\n\n    Spawns daemon threads to evaluate gate criteria on step output files\n    after the step subprocess completes. Results are collected via the\n    internal GateResultQueue.\n\n    Thread safety: submit() and drain() may be called concurrently from\n    any thread. cancel() propagates to all active daemon threads.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, result_queue: GateResultQueue | None = None) -> None:\n        self._queue = result_queue or GateResultQueue()\n        self._threads: list[threading.Thread] = []\n        self._cancelled = threading.Event()\n        self._pending_count = 0\n        self._lock = threading.Lock()\n\n    @property\n    def result_queue(self) -> GateResultQueue:\n        return self._queue\n\n    def submit(\n        self,\n        step: Step,\n        gate_check: Callable[[Path, GateCriteria], tuple[bool, str | None]] = gate_passed,\n    ) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Spawn a daemon thread to evaluate gate criteria on step output.\n\n        The thread terminates after evaluation completes or cancellation.\n        \"\"\"\n        if step.gate is None:\n            # No gate to evaluate; submit a pass result immediately\n            self._queue.put(\n                TrailingGateResult(\n                    step_id=step.id,\n                    passed=True,\n                    evaluation_ms=0.0,\n                    failure_reason=None,\n                )\n            )\n            return\n\n        with self._lock:\n            self._pending_count += 1\n\n        def _evaluate() -> None:\n            try:\n                if self._cancelled.is_set():\n                    return\n                start = time.monotonic()\n                passed, reason = gate_check(step.output_file, step.gate)\n                elapsed_ms = (time.monotonic() - start) * 1000\n                result = TrailingGateResult(\n                    step_id=step.id,\n                    passed=passed,\n                    evaluation_ms=elapsed_ms,\n                    failure_reason=reason,\n                )\n                self._queue.put(result)\n                _log.debug(\n                    \"Trailing gate for '%s': %s (%.1fms)\",\n                    step.id,\n                    \"PASS\" if passed else \"FAIL\",\n                    elapsed_ms,\n                )\n            except Exception:\n                _log.exception(\"Trailing gate evaluation error for step '%s'\", step.id)\n                self._queue.put(\n                    TrailingGateResult(\n                        step_id=step.id,\n                        passed=False,\n                        evaluation_ms=0.0,\n                        failure_reason=\"Gate evaluation raised an exception\",\n                    )\n                )\n            finally:\n                with self._lock:\n                    self._pending_count -= 1\n\n        t = threading.Thread(target=_evaluate, daemon=True)\n        self._threads.append(t)\n        t.start()\n\n    def drain(self) -> list[TrailingGateResult]:\n        \"\"\"Collect all completed gate results.\"\"\"\n        return self._queue.drain()\n\n    def wait_for_pending(self, timeout: float = 30.0) -> list[TrailingGateResult]:\n        \"\"\"Block until all pending gate evaluations complete or timeout.\n\n        Returns all accumulated results. Never hangs indefinitely.\n        \"\"\"\n        deadline = time.monotonic() + timeout\n        # Join all active threads with bounded timeout\n        for t in list(self._threads):\n            remaining = deadline - time.monotonic()\n            if remaining <= 0:\n                _log.warning(\"wait_for_pending timed out with %d threads still active\", self._pending_count)\n                break\n            t.join(timeout=remaining)\n\n        # Drain whatever results are available\n        return self.drain()\n\n    def cancel(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Signal cancellation to all pending daemon threads.\n\n        Threads check the cancellation event and terminate gracefully.\n        \"\"\"\n        self._cancelled.set()\n        # Give threads a brief window to notice cancellation\n        for t in list(self._threads):\n            t.join(timeout=1.0)\n        self._threads.clear()\n\n    @property\n    def pending_count(self) -> int:\n        \"\"\"Number of gate evaluations still in progress.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            return self._pending_count\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# T05.03 --   break\n\n        # 3 producer threads, each producing 10 results\n        threads = [\n            threading.Thread(target=producer, args=(0, 10)),\n            threading.Thread(target=producer, args=(100, 10)),\n            threading.Thread(target=producer, args=(200, 10)),\n        ]\n        for t in threads:\n            t.start()\n        for t in threads:\n            t.join()\n\n        # Drain all results\n        final = q.drain()\n        assert len(final) == 30  # All 30 results collected without loss\n\n    def test_results_associated_with_correct_step_id(self):\n        q.put(TrailingGateResult(step_id=\"beta\", passed=False, evaluation_ms=2.0, failure_reason=\"bad\"))\n        results = q.drain()\n        by_id = {r.step_id: r for r in results}\n             step_id=f\"w-{i}\", passed=False,\n                    evaluation_ms=float(i), failure_reason=f\"fail-{i}\",\n                ))\n\n        def reader():\n            for _ in range(20):\n       r1 = threading.Thread(target=reader)\n        r2 = threading.Thread(target=reader)\n        w.start()\n        r1.start()\n        r2.start()\n        w.join()\n        r1.join()\n        r2.join()\n\n        assert len(errors) == 0\n        assert log.entry_count == 20\n\n\n# ===========================================================================\n# T05.04 -- Scope-Based Gate When no overlap exists, the result\n    is PASSTHROUGH.\n\n    Handles edge cases gracefully:\n    - Empty remediation_files: no conflict possible → PASSTHROUGH\n    - Empty intervening_files: no conflict possible → PASSTHROUGH\n    - Both empty: PASSTHROUGH\n\n    Args:\n        remediation_files: Files modified by the remediation step.\n        intervening_files: Files modified by intervening tasks.\n\n    Returns:\n        ConflictReviewResult with action and overlap details.\n    \"\"\"\n    overlap = detect_file_overlap(remediation_files, intervening_files)\n\n    if overlap:\n        _log.info(\n            \"Conflict review: REGATE required for %d overlapping file(s)\",\n            len(overlap),\n        )\n        return ConflictReviewResult(\n            action=ConflictAction.REGATE,\n            overlapping_files=overlap,\n            remediation_files=remediation_files,\n            intervening_files=intervening_files,\n        )\n\n    _log.debug(\"Conflict review: no overlap, PASSTHROUGH\")\n    return ConflictReviewResult(\n        action=ConflictAction.PASSTHROUGH,\n        overlapping_files=set(),\n        remediation_files=remediation_files,\n        intervening_files=intervening_files,\n    )\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

= \"root_causes\"\n    SOLUTIONS = \"solutions\"\n    SUMMARY = \"summary\"\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass StageResult:\n    \"\"\"Result from a single diagnostic stage.\"\"\"\n\n    stage: DiagnosticStage\n    output: str\n    success: bool = True\n    error: str | None = None\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass DiagnosticReport:\n    \"\"\"Complete diagnostic report from the chain.\"\"\"\n\n    stage_results: list[StageResult] = field(default_factory=list)\n    summary: str = \"\"\n\n    @property\n    def is_complete(self) -> bool:\n        return len(self.stage_results) == 4 and all(\n            r.success for r in self.stage_results\n        )\n\n    @property\n    def stages_completed(self) -> int:\n        return sum(1 for r in self.stage_results if r.success)\n\n    def get_stage(self, stage: DiagnosticStage) -> StageResult | None:\n        for r in self.stage_results:\n            if r.stage == stage:\n                return r\n        return None\n\n\ndef _run_troubleshoot(\n    failure_reason: str,\n    remediation_output: str,\n    step_id: str,\n) -> StageResult:\n    \"\"\"Stage 1: Analyze gate failure and remediation output.\"\"\"\n    analysis = (\n        f\"## Troubleshoot Analysis for '{step_id}'\\n\\n\"\n        f\"### Gate Failure\\n{failure_reason}\\n\\n\"\n        f\"### Remediation Output\\n\"\n        f\"{remediation_output[:500] if remediation_output else '(no output)'}\\n\\n\"\n        f\"### Initial Assessment\\n\"\n        f\"The gate failure indicates: {failure_reason}. \"\n        f\"Remediation was attempted but did not resolve the issue.\"\n    )\n    return StageResult(\n        stage=DiagnosticStage.TROUBLESHOOT,\n        output=analysis,\n    )\n\n\ndef _run_root_causes(\n    troubleshoot_output: str,\n    failure_reason: str,\n) -> StageResult:\n    \"\"\"Stage 2: Generate root cause hypotheses (adversarial).\"\"\"\n    hypotheses = (\n        \"## Root Cause Hypotheses\\n\\n\"\n        \"1. **Primary hypothesis**: The remediation step did not address \"\n        f\"the root cause of: {failure_reason}\\n\"\n        \"2. **Secondary hypothesis**: The acceptance criteria may be \"\n        \"inconsistent with the task requirements\\n\"\n        \"3. **Tertiary hypothesis**: External dependencies or state \"\n        \"changes between attempts may have introduced new failures\\n\"\n    )\n    return StageResult(\n        stage=DiagnosticStage.ROOT_CAUSES,\n        output=hypotheses,\n    )\n\n\ndef _run_solutions(\n    root_causes_output: str,\n    step_id: str,\n) -> StageResult:\n    \"\"\"Stage 3: Generate solution proposals (adversarial).\"\"\"\n    solutions = (\n        \"## Proposed Solutions\\n\\n\"\n        f\"For step '{step_id}':\\n\"\n        \"1. **Manual intervention**: Review the gate criteria and adjust \"\n        \"if they are too strict for the current context\\n\"\n        \"2. **Targeted fix**: Address each root cause hypothesis individually \"\n        \"with focused corrections\\n\"\n        \"3. **Decomposition**: Break the step into smaller sub-steps \"\n        \"that can be gated independently\\n\"\n    )\n    return StageResult(\n        stage=DiagnosticStage.SOLUTIONS,\n        output=solutions,\n    )\n\n\ndef _run_summary(\n    stages: list[StageResult],\n    step_id: str,\n) -> StageResult:\n    \"\"\"Stage 4: Compile chain output into actionable report.\"\"\"\n    successful = [s for s in stages if s.success]\n    failed = [s for s in stages if not s.success]\n\n    parts = [\n        f\"# Diagnostic Summary for '{step_id}'\\n\",\n        f\"Stages completed: {len(successful)}/{len(stages)}\\n\",\n    ]\n\n    for stage in successful:\n        parts.append(f\"\\n{stage.output}\\n\")\n\n    if failed:\n        parts.append(\"\\n## Degraded Stages\\n\")\n        for stage in failed:\n            parts.append(f\"- {stage.stage.value}: {stage.error}\\n\")\n\n    summary_text = \"\\n\".join(parts)\n    return StageResult(\n        stage=DiagnosticStage.SUMMARY,\n        output=summary_text,\n    )\n\n\ndef run_diagnostic_chain(\n    step_id: str,\n    failure_reason: str,\n    remediation_output: str = \"\",\n) -> DiagnosticReport:\n    \"\"\"Execute the full diagnostic chain with graceful degradation.\n\n    Each stage catches exceptions and returns partial results. Subsequent\n    stages receive whatever partial output is available.\n\n    This is runner-side execution: no TurnLedger turns consumed (Gap 2).\n\n    Args:\n        step_id: The step that persistently failed.\n        failure_reason: The gate failure reason.\n        remediation_output: Output from the failed remediation attempts.\n\n    Returns:\n        DiagnosticReport with all stage results and summary.\n    \"\"\"\n    report = DiagnosticReport()\n\n    # Stage 1: Troubleshoot\n    try:\n        troubleshoot = _run_troubleshoot(failure_reason, remediation_output, step_id)\n        report.stage_results.append(troubleshoot)\n    except Exception as e:\n        _log.warning(\"Diagnostic stage TROUBLESHOOT failed: %s\", e)\n        troubleshoot = StageResult(\n            stage=DiagnosticStage.TROUBLESHOOT,\n            output=\"\", success=False, error=str(e),\n        )\n        report.stage_results.append(troubleshoot)\n\n    # Stage 2: Root causes\n    try:\n        root_causes = _run_root_causes(\n            troubleshoot.output if troubleshoot.success else \"\",\n            failure_reason,\n        )\n        report.stage_results.append(root_causes)\n    except Exception as e:\n        _log.warning(\"Diagnostic stage ROOT_CAUSES failed: %s\", e)\n        root_causes = StageResult(\n            stage=DiagnosticStage.ROOT_CAUSES,\n            output=\"\", success=False, error=str(e),\n        )\n        report.stage_results.append(root_causes)\n\n    # Stage 4: Summary\n    try:\n        summary = _run_summary(report.stage_results, step_id)\n        report.stage_results.append(summary)\n        report.summary = summary.output\n    except Exception as e:\n        _log.warning(\"Diagnostic stage SUMMARY failed: %s\", e)\n        report.stage_results.append(StageResult(\n            stage=DiagnosticStage.SUMMARY,\n            output=\"\", success=False, error=str(e),\n        ))\n\n    return report\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1081,"cache_read_input_tokens":124013,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":1081,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"536630d3-b5df-4d08-ad3e-8d2b6f9b9b0e","uuid":"9e9e1edb-020e-4e4d-a2aa-5da1b15bff5e"}
